///__constant__ const float pi =3.141526;
///__constant__ const float pai=3.141526;

/// first  order: coe[ij +1 ] * 
/// second order: coe[ 0 ] +  coe[ ij ] * (* + *)
/// x axis is the fisrt dimension of input array





extern "C" __global__ void dx_1D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, float spatial_interval, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;

                in_idx = ix;

                float sum=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                    sum = sum + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]);
 
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sum * spatial_interval;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dx_1D_back(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, float spatial_interval, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;

                in_idx = ix;

                float sum=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                    sum = sum + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)]);
 
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sum * spatial_interval;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dxx_1D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, float spatial_interval, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;

                in_idx = ix;

                float sum = coe[0] * input[in_idx];

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                    sum = sum + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]);
 
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sum * spatial_interval;
        }
}

extern "C" __global__ void grad_2D_forw(float* input, float* output1, float* output2, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]); //ij+1           -(ij)

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]); //ij+1           -(ij)
                }

                output1[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx;

                output2[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void div_2D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]); //ij+1           -(ij)

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]); //ij+1           -(ij)
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx + 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}

				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;

                }

        }

extern "C" __global__ void dz_2D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;
                
                float    sumz=0.0f;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]); //ij+1           -(ij)
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}

                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)

                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)]); //+ij           -(ij+1)

        }
}


extern "C" __global__ void div_2D_back(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)]); //+ij           -(ij+1)

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)*dimx]); //+ij           -(ij+1)

                    //sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * ( s_data1[tz][tx + (ij)] - s_data1[tz][tx - (ij+1)] ); //+ij           -(ij+1)

                    //sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * ( s_data1[tz + (ij)][tx] - s_data1[tz - (ij+1)][tx] );  //+ij           -(ij+1)
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx + 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}

extern "C" __global__ void dxx_2D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                sumx = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                sumz = sumx;
                
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]); 
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx;  // *  d x *  d x, this is an error
        }
}


extern "C" __global__ void dzz_2D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;

				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;;

extern "C" __global__ void lap_2D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                sumx = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                sumz = sumx;
                
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]); 

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] + input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx + 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}


extern "C" __global__ void lap_2D_double(double* input, double* output, double* coe, int dimx, int dimz, double dx, double dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if ((ix < dimx) && (iz < dimz))
        {
                dimx = dimx + 2 * radius;
                dimz = dimz + 2 * radius;

                ix = ix + radius;
                iz = iz + radius;

                in_idx = iz * dimx + ix;  // ix * dimz + iz;;

                double sumx = 0.0, sumz = 0.0;

                sumx = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                sumz = sumx;

                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]);

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij) * dimx] + input[in_idx - (ij) * dimx]);
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0 * sumx * dx + 1.0 * sumz * dz;
        }
}

extern "C" __global__ void grad_2D(float* input, float* output1, float* output2, float* coe, int dimx, int dimz, float dx, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iz = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int in_idx;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
				in_idx = iz*dimx+ix; //ix*dimz+iz;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]); //ij+1           -(ij)

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]); //ij+1           -(ij)
                }

                output1[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumx * dx;

                output2[in_idx] = 1.0f * sumz * dz;
        }
}

Key: D3_kernel, Value: 



__constant__ const float pi =3.141526;
__constant__ const float pai=3.141526;




extern "C" __global__ void grad_3D_forw(float* input, float* output1, float* output2, float* output3, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumy=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]);//[nz, ny, nx], nx

                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);//[nz, ny, nx], ny

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimxdimy] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimxdimy]);//[nz, ny, nx], nz
                }

                output1[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx;
                output2[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumy * dy;
                output3[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void div_3D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumy=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]);

                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimxdimy] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimxdimy]);
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx + 1.0f *  sumy * dy + 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dx_3D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]);
                

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dy_3D_forw(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dy, int radius)
{

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij+1)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumy * dy;
        }
}

extern "C" __global__ void grad_3D_back(float* input, float* output1, float* output2, float* output3, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumy=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 0; ij <= radius-1; ij++)
                {
                     sumx = sumx + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)]); 

                     sumy = sumy + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)*dimx]);

                     sumz = sumz + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimxdimy] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)*dimxdimy]);
                }

                output1[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx;
                output2[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumy * dy;
                output3[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void div_3D_back(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)

        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;

                     sumy = sumy + coe[ij+1] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij+1)*dimx]);

extern "C" __global__ void dxx_3D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;

                float    sumx=0.0f;
                
                sumx = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]);
                
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dyy_3D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dy, int radius)

                dimz=dimz+2*radius;

                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;

                float    sumy=0.0f;
                
                sumy = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] + input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);
                
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumy * dy;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dzz_3D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;

                float    sumz=0.0f;
                
                sumz = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimxdimy] + input[in_idx - (ij)*dimxdimy]);
                
                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void lap_3D(float* input, float* output, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;

                float    sumx=0.0f, sumy=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;
                sumx = coe[0] * input[in_idx];
                sumy = sumx;
                sumz = sumx;
                
                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] + input[in_idx - (ij)]);
                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] + input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);
                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimxdimy] + input[in_idx - (ij)*dimxdimy]);
                }

                output[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx + 1.0f *  sumy * dy + 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}



extern "C" __global__ void grad_3D(float* input, float* output1, float* output2, float* output3, float* coe, int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, float dx, float dy, float dz, int radius)
{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;
        int iz = blockIdx.z*blockDim.z+threadIdx.z;
        
        int in_idx;
        int dimxdimy;

        if((ix<dimx)&&(iy<dimy)&&(iz<dimz))
		{
                dimx=dimx+2*radius;
                dimy=dimy+2*radius;
                dimz=dimz+2*radius;
				
                ix=ix+radius;
                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;
                
                dimxdimy = dimx*dimy;
				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;
                
                float    sumx=0.0f, sumy=0.0f, sumz=0.0f;

                //#pragma unroll
                for (int ij = 1; ij <= radius; ij++)
                {
                    sumx = sumx + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)] - input[in_idx - (ij)]);//[nz, ny, nx], nx

                    sumy = sumy + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimx] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimx]);//[nz, ny, nx], ny

                    sumz = sumz + coe[ij] * (input[in_idx + (ij)*dimxdimy] - input[in_idx - (ij)*dimxdimy]);//[nz, ny, nx], nz
                }

                output1[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumx * dx;
                output2[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumy * dy;
                output3[in_idx] = 1.0f *  sumz * dz;
        }
}

{
        int ix = blockIdx.x*blockDim.x+threadIdx.x;
        int iy = blockIdx.y*blockDim.y+threadIdx.y;

                dimz=dimz+2*radius;

                iy=iy+radius;
                iz=iz+radius;

				in_idx = iz*dimxdimy + iy*dimx +ix;

Key: wave_kernel, Value: 
__constant__ const float pi =3.141526;
__constant__ const float pai=3.141526;
__constant__ const float share_zero=0;


extern "C" __global__ void add_source_signal_kernel_2D(
    float* p2,              
    const int* sx_arr,      
    const int* sz_arr,      
    const float* signal,                 
    int nx,                 
    int nz,                 
    int ns,
    int accumulation                  
)
{
    int idx = blockDim.x * blockIdx.x + threadIdx.x;
    if (idx < ns)
    {
        int iz     = sz_arr[idx];
        int ix     = sx_arr[idx];
        int index  = iz * nx + ix;
        
        if(accumulation)
        {
            atomicAdd(&p2[index], signal[idx]);
        }
        else
        {
            p2[index] = signal[idx];
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void add_source_signal_kernel_3D(
    float* p2,              
    const int* sx_arr,
    const int* sy_arr,      
    const int* sz_arr,      
    const float* signal,                 
    int nx,
    int ny,                 
    int nz,                 
    int ns,
    int add_mark                  
)
{
    int idx = blockDim.x * blockIdx.x + threadIdx.x;
    if (idx < ns)
    {
        int iz     = sz_arr[idx];
        int iy     = sy_arr[idx];
        int ix     = sx_arr[idx];

        int index  = iz * ny * nx + iy * nx + ix;
        
        if(add_mark)
        {
            atomicAdd(&p2[index], signal[idx]);
        }
        else
        {
            p2[index] = signal[idx];
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mul_a_b_to_c_1D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] * backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_add_a_b_to_c_1D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] + backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_sub_a_b_to_c_1D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] - backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_div_a_b_to_c_1D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        if(backward_p[idx]!=0)
            output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] / backward_p[idx] );
        else
            output[idx] = 0.0;
    }
}


extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mul_a_b_to_c_1D_add(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        ///You need to set the zero at out of loop in the main code;
        output[idx] += 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] * backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_add_a_b_to_c_1D_add(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        ///You need to set the zero at out of loop in the main code;
        output[idx] += 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] + backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_sub_a_b_to_c_1D_add(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        ///You need to set the zero at out of loop in the main code;
        output[idx] += 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] - backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_div_a_b_to_c_1D_add(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        ///You need to set the zero at out of loop in the main code;
        if(backward_p[idx]!=0)
            output[idx] += 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] / backward_p[idx] );
        else
            output[idx] = 0.0;
    }
}


extern "C" __global__ void acoustic_poynting_shared_3D(
    float* p, float* vx, float* vy, float* vz, 
    float* px, float* py, float* pz, 
    int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, 
    int radius1, int radius2, int radius3) 
{

    //static_assert(sizeof(float) == 4, "Data type is not float.");
    //static_assert(sizeof(int) == 4, "Data type is not int.");

    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    int in_idx;
    int ou_idx;
    int dimxdimy = dimx * dimy;

    // Make sure the indices are within valid bounds, avoiding boundary issues
    if ((ix < dimx - 2 * radius1) && (iy < dimy - 2 * radius2) && (iz < dimz - 2 * radius3)) 
    {

        ix = ix + radius1;
        iy = iy + radius2;
        iz = iz + radius3;

        ou_idx = iz * dimxdimy + iy * dimx + ix;

        float sumx = 0.0f, sumy = 0.0f, sumz = 0.0f;

        //#pragma unroll
        for (int i = -radius1; i <= radius1; i++) 
        {
            for (int j = -radius2; j <= radius2; j++) 
            {
                for (int k = -radius3; k <= radius3; k++) 
                {
                    // Compute input index with proper strides in all 3 dimensions
                    in_idx = ou_idx + k * dimxdimy + j * dimx + i;

                    // Correct Poynting vector component calculations
                    sumx = sumx + p[in_idx] * vx[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in x-direction
                    sumy = sumy + p[in_idx] * vy[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in y-direction
                    sumz = sumz + p[in_idx] * vz[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in z-direction
                }
            }
        }

        // Store the results with a scaling factor of -1
        px[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumx;
        py[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumy;
        pz[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumz;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void acoustic_poynting_global_3D(
    float* p, float* vx, float* vy, float* vz, 
    float* px, float* py, float* pz, 
    int dimx, int dimy, int dimz, 
    int radius1, int radius2, int radius3) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    int in_idx;
    int ou_idx;
    int dimxdimy = dimx * dimy;

    // Make sure the indices are within valid bounds, avoiding boundary issues
    if ((ix < dimx - 2 * radius1) && (iy < dimy - 2 * radius2) && (iz < dimz - 2 * radius3)) 
    {

        ix = ix + radius1;
        iy = iy + radius2;
        iz = iz + radius3;

        ou_idx = iz * dimxdimy + iy * dimx + ix;

        float sumx = 0.0f, sumy = 0.0f, sumz = 0.0f;

        //#pragma unroll
        for (int i = -radius1; i <= radius1; i++) 
        {
            for (int j = -radius2; j <= radius2; j++) 
            {
                for (int k = -radius3; k <= radius3; k++) 
                {
                    // Compute input index with proper strides in all 3 dimensions
                    in_idx = ou_idx + k * dimxdimy + j * dimx + i;

                    // Correct Poynting vector component calculations
                    sumx = sumx + p[in_idx] * vx[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in x-direction
                    sumy = sumy + p[in_idx] * vy[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in y-direction
                    sumz = sumz + p[in_idx] * vz[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in z-direction
                }
            }
        }

        // Store the results with a scaling factor of -1
        px[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumx;
        py[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumy;
        pz[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumz;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void acoustic_poynting_global_2D(
    float* p, float* vx, float* vz, 
    float* px, float* pz, 
    int dimx, int dimz, 
    int radius1, int radius3) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;


    int in_idx;
    int ou_idx;


    // Make sure the indices are within valid bounds, avoiding boundary issues
    if ((ix < dimx - 2 * radius1) && (iz < dimz - 2 * radius3)) 
    {

        ix = ix + radius1;
       
        iz = iz + radius3;

        ou_idx = iz * dimx + ix;

        float sumx = 0.0f, sumz = 0.0f;

        //#pragma unroll
        for (int i = -radius1; i <= radius1; i++) 
        {
           
                for (int k = -radius3; k <= radius3; k++) 
                {
                    // Compute input index with proper strides in all 3 dimensions
                    in_idx = ou_idx + k * dimx + i;

                    // Correct Poynting vector component calculations
                    sumx = sumx + p[in_idx] * vx[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in x-direction
                    
                    sumz = sumz + p[in_idx] * vz[in_idx];  // Poynting vector in z-direction
                }
            
        }

        // Store the results with a scaling factor of -1
        px[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumx;

        pz[ou_idx] = -1.0f * sumz;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_amp_time_abs_3D(float* p3, float* ex_amp_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int ny, int nz, int it) 
{

    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        if ( fabs(p3[idx]) >= fabs(ex_amp_d[idx]) ) 
        {
            ex_amp_d[idx]  = p3[idx];
            ex_time_d[idx] = (float)it;
        }
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_amp_time_abs_2D(float* p3, float* ex_amp_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int nz, int it) 
{

    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;


    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * nx + ix;

        if ( fabs(p3[idx]) >= fabs(ex_amp_d[idx]) ) 
        {
            ex_amp_d[idx]  = p3[idx];
            ex_time_d[idx] = (float)it;
        }
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_amp_time_3D(float* p3, float* ex_amp_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int ny, int nz, int it)

    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        if ( (p3[idx]) >= (ex_amp_d[idx]) ) 
        {
            ex_amp_d[idx]  = p3[idx];
            ex_time_d[idx] = (float)it;
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_get_array_at_time_3D(float* p3, float* ex_amp_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int ny, int nz, int it) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        if (ex_time_d[idx] == (float)it) 
        {
            ex_amp_d[idx] = p3[idx];
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_amp_time_abs_1D(float* p3, float* ex_amp_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int it) 
{

    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        int idx = ix;

        if ( fabs(p3[idx]) >= fabs(ex_amp_d[idx]) ) 
        {
            ex_amp_d[idx]  = fabs(p3[idx]);
            ex_time_d[idx] = (float)it;
        }
    }
}

    {

        if ( (p3[idx]) >= (ex_amp_d[idx]) )

        }
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_get_array_at_time_1D(float* input_d, float* output_d, float* ex_time_d, int nx, int it) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        int idx = ix;

        if (ex_time_d[idx] == (float)it) 
        {
            output_d[idx] = input_d[idx];
        }
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dt_3D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *output, int nx, int ny, int nz, float rep_dt) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * (current_arr[idx] - previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dt;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dt_2D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *output, int nx, int nz, float rep_dt) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * (current_arr[idx] - previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dt;
    }
}




extern "C" __global__ void dt_1D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *output, int nx, float rep_dt)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * (current_arr[idx] - previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dt;
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cross_correlation_IC_2D_part(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx, int nz, int bl, int bu, int nnx, int nnz)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        int ou_idx  = iz * nx + ix;
        int in_idx = (iz + bu) * nnx + ix + bl;
        output[ou_idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[in_idx] * backward_p[in_idx] );
    }
}





extern "C" __global__ void cross_correlation_IC_1D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] * backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cross_correlation_IC_2D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx, int nz)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] * backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cross_correlation_IC_3D(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx, int ny, int nz)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[idx] * backward_p[idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cross_correlation_IC_3D_part(float *forward_p, float *backward_p, float *output, int nx, int ny, int nz, int bl, int bb, int bu, int nnx, int nny, int nnz)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int ou_idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;
        int in_idx = (iz + bu) * (nnx * nny) + (iy + bb) * nnx + ix + bl;

        output[ou_idx] = 1.0f * ( forward_p[in_idx] * backward_p[in_idx] );
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void dtdt_3D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *further_arr, float *output, int nx, int ny, int nz, float rep_dtdt) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * (nx * ny) + iy * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * (further_arr[idx] - 2.0*current_arr[idx] + previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dtdt;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void dtdt_2D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *further_arr, float *output, int nx, int nz, float rep_dtdt) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        int idx = iz * nx + ix;

        output[idx] = 1.0f * (further_arr[idx] - 2.0*current_arr[idx] + previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dtdt;
    }
}




extern "C" __global__ void dtdt_1D(float *previous_arr, float *current_arr, float *further_arr, float *output, int nx, float rep_dtdt)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx) 
    {
        output[idx] = 1.0f * (further_arr[idx] - 2.0*current_arr[idx] + previous_arr[idx]) * rep_dtdt;
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_form_Toeplitz_matrix_2D(float *intput_d, float *output_d, int nx, int lt) 
{
    ///there is no flip the input in out of function
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    int half_lt = int(lt/2);

    if ( ix < nx && iy < lt && iz < lt ) 
    {
        int ou_idx = iz * (nx * lt) + iy * nx + ix;  //output [lt, lt, nx]

        int iit    = iz - iy + half_lt;

        if ( iit >=0 && iit<lt )
        {
            int in_idx = ( iit ) * nx + ix; //intput_d  [lt, nx]
            output_d[ou_idx] = intput_d[in_idx];
        }   
        else 
        {
            output_d[ou_idx] = 0.0f; 
        } 
    }
}

//     for it = 1 : nz

//             output(iz,it)=0.0;
//             in_idx=iz-it+1+floor(nz/2);

//             end

////the final parameter is for accumulation
////the final parameter is for accumulation
extern "C" __global__ void acoustic_kichhoff_modeling_adjoint_source_ND(

       float *N_scattering_source,
       float *first_derivative_p,
       float *angle_ref_d,
       float *half_scattering_angle_d,
       int nx,

       float angle_start,
       float angle_interval,
       int angle_num,
       float angle_sigma,

       int angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool,
       int accumulation
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {

        // Compute the half opening angle and angle scale
        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];

        // Reference value based on angle index
        float angle_scale = 0.0f;
        float ref = 0.0f;

        if(angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool)
        {
            angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//cos(	heta)

            // Determine the angle index
            int i_angle = int((half_opening_angle12 - angle_start) / angle_interval);
            if (i_angle >= 0 && i_angle < angle_num) 
            {
                ref = angle_ref_d[i_angle * nx + in_idx12];  // 3D reference lookup
            }
            else
            {
                ref = angle_ref_d[(angle_num-1) * nx + in_idx12];//default we will use the final or we do not simulate the data using large angle, that is we must remove the diving wave in the observed data from two-way equation
            }
        } 
        else
        {
            angle_scale = 1.0f;
            ref = angle_ref_d[in_idx12];
        }

        if(accumulation)
        {
            //N_scattering_source[in_idx12] += first_derivative_p[in_idx12] * angle_scale * ref; /// there is no scale, you can compute out of the kernel
            atomicAdd(&N_scattering_source[in_idx12], first_derivative_p[in_idx12] * angle_scale * ref);
        }
        else
        {
            N_scattering_source[in_idx12] = first_derivative_p[in_idx12] * angle_scale * ref;
        }
    }
}



////born_rel_vel = Delta v / v   = 2 * r( 	hea ) * cos( 	hea )^2 
extern "C" __global__ void acoustic_relative_vp_from_band_limited_angle_dependent_reflectivity_ND(

       float *output_d,
       float *born_rel_vel_d,
       float *angle_ref_d,
       float *half_scattering_angle_d,
       int nx,

       float angle_start,
       float angle_interval,
       int angle_num,
       float angle_sigma
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {

        // Compute the half opening angle and angle scale
        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];

        // Reference value based on angle index
        float angle_scale = 0.0f;
        float ref = 0.0f;

        
        angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 2.0f);

        // Determine the angle index
        int i_angle = int((half_opening_angle12 - angle_start) / angle_interval);
        if (i_angle >= 0 && i_angle < angle_num) 
        {
            ref = angle_ref_d[i_angle * nx + in_idx12];
            output_d[in_idx12] = 2.0 * ref * angle_scale;
        }
        else
        {
            output_d[in_idx12] = born_rel_vel_d[in_idx12];
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void vector_normalized_2D(
    float *px_d,
    float *pz_d,
    float *normalized_px_d,
    float *normalized_pz_d,
    int nx,
    float epsilon
)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (idx < nx)
    {
        float px = px_d[idx];
        float pz = pz_d[idx];

        // Compute vector magnitude with epsilon to avoid divide-by-zero
        float mag = sqrtf(px * px + pz * pz + epsilon);

        normalized_px_d[idx] = px / mag;
        normalized_pz_d[idx] = pz / mag;
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void vector_to_angle_z_sin_2D(
    float *px_d,
    float *pz_d,
    float *angle_d,
    int     nx,
    float epsilon
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
            float norm        = sqrtf(px_d[in_idx12]*px_d[in_idx12] + pz_d[in_idx12]*pz_d[in_idx12]);
            float sin_theta=0.0f;

            if(norm!=0)
            {
                sin_theta   = px_d[in_idx12] / (norm + epsilon);
            }
            
            /////there is no  divide 2
            if ( fabsf(sin_theta) < 1.0f )
                angle_d[in_idx12]  = float(asinf(sin_theta) * 180.0f / pi);
            else
                angle_d[in_idx12]  = 0.0f;
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void vector_to_angle_z_cos_2D(
    float *px_d,
    float *pz_d,
    float *angle_d,
    int     nx,
    float epsilon
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
            float norm        = sqrtf(px_d[in_idx12]*px_d[in_idx12] + pz_d[in_idx12]*pz_d[in_idx12]);
            float cos_theta=0.0f;

            if(norm!=0)
            {
                cos_theta   = pz_d[in_idx12] / (norm + epsilon);
            }
            
            /////there is no  divide 2
            if ( fabsf(cos_theta) < 1.0f )
                angle_d[in_idx12]  = float(acosf(cos_theta) * 180.0f / pi);
            else
                angle_d[in_idx12]  = 0.0f;
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void vector_to_angle_z_tan_2D(
    float *px_d,
    float *pz_d,
    float *angle_d,
    int     nx,
    float epsilon
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
            float tan_theta=0.0f;

            if(pz_d[in_idx12]!=0)
            {
                tan_theta           = px_d[in_idx12] / pz_d[in_idx12];
                angle_d[in_idx12]   = float(atanf(tan_theta) * 180.0f / pi) ;
            }
            else
            {
                angle_d[in_idx12]   = 0.0f;
            }
    }
}


extern "C" __global__ void cuda_nan_inf_to_zero(
    float *input_arr_d,
    int nx
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
        float val = input_arr_d[in_idx12];

        // First check for NaN
        if (isnan(val) || isinf(val))
        {
            input_arr_d[in_idx12] = 0.0f;  // or set to 0.0f if you prefer
        }
        
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_kernel_clip_and_nan_inf(
    float *input_arr_d,
    int nx,
    float min_value,
    float max_value
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
        float val = input_arr_d[in_idx12];

        if (isnan(val) || isinf(val))
        {
            input_arr_d[in_idx12] = 0.0f;  // or 0.0f
        }
        else
        {
            if (val < min_value)
            {
                input_arr_d[in_idx12] = min_value;
            }

            if (val > max_value)
            {
                input_arr_d[in_idx12] = max_value;
            }
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_kernel_clip(
    float *input_arr_d,
    int nx,
    float min_value,
    float max_value
)
{
    int in_idx12 = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;

    if (in_idx12 < nx) 
    {
        if (input_arr_d[in_idx12] < min_value)
        {
            input_arr_d[in_idx12] = min_value;
        }

        if (input_arr_d[in_idx12] > max_value)
        {
            input_arr_d[in_idx12] = max_value;
        }
    }
}

// d = A1 * A2 * f(t-T1-T2) * [    born_rel_K / K + born_rel_den_d*cos(2 * \cita) /K      ]
// if para_dependent_compensate_mark == 0:  scale=1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_modeling_multi_parameter_2D(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length,

    int lt,

    float *total_acc_d, 
    float *s_amp_d,
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d,
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr,
    float *born_rel_vel_d, 
    float *born_rel_den_d,

    int para_dependent_compensate_mark,
    int it_beg, 
    int it_end, 
    int nx, 
    int nz,

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power
) 
{
    // Get the 3D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int im = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    // Calculate 1D index for 2D array
    int in_idx12 = iz * nx + ix;
    int nxnynz = nx * nz;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz && im < (it_end - it_beg)) 
    {
        int it = it_beg + im;  // Calculate time index

        // Perform calculations
        float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Receiver amplitude
        int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Receiver time
        float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Source amplitude
        int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Source time

        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];  // Half scattering angle
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(2.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f); //this is 2.0f times half_opening_angle12  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2

        float born_rel_K = born_rel_den_d[in_idx12] + 2.0f * born_rel_vel_d[in_idx12];

        // Conditional check for parameter-dependent compensation
        float K = 1.0f;
        if (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) 
        {
            K = p_vel_arr[in_idx12] * p_vel_arr[in_idx12] * den_arr[in_idx12];
        }

        float scale1 = born_rel_K / K;
        float scale2 = (born_rel_den_d[in_idx12] / K) * angle_scale;

        // Calculate time index in the wavelet
        int f_it = int(it - T1 - T2 + wavelet_length);

        // Apply the source function if within bounds
        if (f_it < wavelet_length && f_it >= 0) 
        {
            float f_value = source_func[f_it];  
            int out_idx;
            out_idx = im * nxnynz + in_idx12;
            total_acc_d[ out_idx ] = A1 * A2 * f_value * (scale1 + scale2);
        }
    }
}




// d = A1 * A2 * f(t-T1-T2) * [    2 * cos(\cita) * R(x, \cita) / vel      ]
// if para_dependent_compensate_mark == 0:  scale=1.0,  that is 2/v=1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_angle_kirchhoff_modeling_2D(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length,

    int lt,

    float *total_acc_d, 
    float *s_amp_d,
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d,
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    float *angle_ref_d, 

    int para_dependent_compensate_mark,
    int it_beg, 
    int it_end, 
    int nx, 
    int nz, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,
    int angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool
) 
{
    // 3D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int im = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    // Calculate 1D index for 2D array
    int in_idx12 = iz * nx + ix;
    int nxnynz = nx * nz;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz && im < (it_end - it_beg)) 
    {
        int it = it_beg + im;  // Time index

        // Load values for amplitudes and times
        float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Receiver amplitude
        int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Receiver time
        float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Source amplitude
        int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Source time

        // Compute the half opening angle and angle scale
        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];

        // Reference value based on angle index
        float angle_scale = 0.0f;
        float ref = 0.0f;

        if(angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool)
        {
            angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//this is 1.0f times half_opening_angle12  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2

            // Determine the angle index
            int i_angle = int((half_opening_angle12 - angle_start) / angle_interval);
            if (i_angle >= 0 && i_angle < angle_num) 
            {
                ref = angle_ref_d[i_angle * nxnynz + in_idx12];  // 3D reference lookup
            }
        } 
        else
        {
            angle_scale = 1.0f;
            ref = angle_ref_d[in_idx12];
        }

        // Parameter-dependent compensation
        float para_scale = 1.0f;
        if (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) 
        {
            para_scale = 2.0f / (p_vel_arr[in_idx12]);
        }

        // Calculate the time index in the wavelet
        int f_it = int(it - T1 - T2 + wavelet_length);

        // Apply source function if within bounds
        if (f_it < wavelet_length && f_it >= 0) 
        {
            float f_value = source_func[f_it];

            int out_idx;
            out_idx = im * nxnynz + in_idx12;

            total_acc_d[ out_idx ] = A1 * A2 * f_value * ref * para_scale * angle_scale;
        }
    }
}


//////////////////
//////////////////
//////////////////
//////////////////
//////////////////
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_Fresnel_zone(
    float *Fresnel_zone_arr, 
    int nx, 
    float Fresnel_angle_len, 
    float *normal_angle_d, 
    float *source_propagation_angle_d, 
    float *receiver_propagation_angle_d,
    float *normal_propagation_angle_d
)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;
        float s_cita1 = (source_propagation_angle_d[in_idx34]   - normal_angle_d[in_idx34]);
        float r_cita1 = (-receiver_propagation_angle_d[in_idx34]+ normal_angle_d[in_idx34]);
       
        float delta_cita1  = fabs(s_cita1 - r_cita1);
        float delta_cita2  = fabs( normal_propagation_angle_d[in_idx34] - normal_angle_d[in_idx34]);

        if(delta_cita1<=Fresnel_angle_len && delta_cita2< Fresnel_angle_len)
        {
            Fresnel_zone_arr[in_idx34] = 1.0;
        }
        else
        {
            Fresnel_zone_arr[in_idx34] = 0;
        }
    }
}
