//mig_K   = 1/K  *  A3 * A4 * f(t-T3-T4);
//mig_rou = 1/K  *  A3 * A4 * f(t-T3-T4) * cos(2 * cita);
//mig_K + mig_rou  = 1/K  *  A3 * A4 * f(t-T3-T4) *  ( 1  + cos(2 * cita) ) = cos(cita)^2

// if there is no para_dependent_compensate_mark, the scale is 1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_multi_parameter_1D_cc(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 
    
    int lt, 

    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *migrated_image2_d, 
    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 
    int nx, 
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,

    float *shot_recording_arr, 
    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff
) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx ) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;

        float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];
        
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(2.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//this is 2.0f times half_opening_angle34  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2 /// 2 times for born, one times for kirchhoff
        
        float K = (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) ? p_vel_arr[in_idx34] * p_vel_arr[in_idx34] * den_arr[in_idx34] : 1.0f;
        
        float scale1 = 1.0f / K;
        float scale2 = (1.0f / K) * angle_scale;
        
        float tmp1 = 0.0f, f_value=0.0f, d_value=0.0f;

        for (int f_it = 0; f_it < wavelet_length; f_it++) 
        {
            int d_it = int(T3 + T4 + f_it - wavelet_length);
            if (d_it < lt && d_it >= 0) 
            {
                f_value = source_func[f_it];
                d_value = shot_recording_arr[d_it];
                
                if (division_mark!=0) 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 / (A4 + stable_coeff) * f_value * d_value;
                } 
                else 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 * A4 * f_value * d_value;
                }
            }
        }
        
        migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
        migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;

        //线程安全性：从线程安全的角度来看，多个线程同时访问 shot_recording_arr[d_it] 中相同的元素是不会引发数据竞争问题的，因为这里涉及的是只读操作。所以，这个函数在读取 shot_recording_arr[d_it] 时是安全的。
    }
}




extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_multi_parameter_1D_de(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 
    
    int lt, 

    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *migrated_image2_d, 
    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 
    int nx, 
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,

    float *shot_recording_arr, 
    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff
) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx ) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;

        float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];
        
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(2.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//this is 2.0f times half_opening_angle34  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2 /// 2 times for born, one times for kirchhoff
        
        float K = (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) ? p_vel_arr[in_idx34] * p_vel_arr[in_idx34] * den_arr[in_idx34] : 1.0f;
        
        float scale1 = 1.0f / K;
        float scale2 = (1.0f / K) * angle_scale;
        
        float tmp1 = 0.0f, f_value=0.0f, d_value=0.0f;

        //for (int f_it = 0; f_it < wavelet_length; f_it++) 
        int f_it=wavelet_max_length;
        {
            int d_it = int(T3 + T4 + f_it - wavelet_length);
            if (d_it < lt && d_it >= 0) 
            {
                f_value = 1.0f;//source_func[f_it];
                d_value = shot_recording_arr[d_it];
                
                if (division_mark!=0) 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 / (A4 + stable_coeff) * f_value * d_value;
                } 
                else 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 * A4 * f_value * d_value;
                }
            }
        }
        
        migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
        migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;

        //线程安全性：从线程安全的角度来看，多个线程同时访问 shot_recording_arr[d_it] 中相同的元素是不会引发数据竞争问题的，因为这里涉及的是只读操作。所以，这个函数在读取 shot_recording_arr[d_it] 时是安全的。
    }
}

//mig_kirchhoff1      = 2/v_x  * A3 * A4 * f(t-T3-T4);
//mig_kirchhoff2      = 2/v_x  * A3 * A4 * f(t-T3-T4) * cos(\cita);

// if there is no para_dependent_compensate_mark, the scale is 1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_kirchhoff_1D_cc(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 
    
    int lt, 
    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *migrated_image2_d, 
    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 
    int nx, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,

    float *shot_recording_arr, 
    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff
) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;

        float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];
        
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f); //this is 1.0f times half_opening_angle34  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2
        
        float inv_K = (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) ? 2.0f / p_vel_arr[in_idx34] : 1.0f;

        float scale1 = inv_K;
        float scale2 = inv_K * angle_scale;
        
        float tmp1 = 0.0f, f_value=0.0f, d_value=0.0f;
        
        for (int f_it = 0; f_it < wavelet_length; f_it++) 
        {
            int d_it = int(T3 + T4 + f_it - wavelet_length);
            if (d_it < lt && d_it >= 0) 
            {
                f_value = source_func[f_it];
                d_value = shot_recording_arr[d_it];
                
                if (division_mark!=0) 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 / (A4 + stable_coeff) * f_value * d_value;
                } else 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 * A4 * f_value * d_value;
                }
            }
        }
        
        //migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
        //migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;

        migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;
        migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_kirchhoff_1D_de(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 
    
    int lt, 
    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *migrated_image2_d, 
    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 
    int nx, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,

    float *shot_recording_arr, 
    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff
) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;

        float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];
        
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f); //this is 1.0f times half_opening_angle34  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2
        
        float inv_K = (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) ? 2.0f / p_vel_arr[in_idx34] : 1.0f;

        float scale1 = inv_K;
        float scale2 = inv_K * angle_scale;
        
        float tmp1 = 0.0f, f_value=0.0f, d_value=0.0f;
        
        //for (int f_it = 0; f_it < wavelet_length; f_it++) 
        int f_it=wavelet_max_length;
        {
            int d_it = int(T3 + T4 + f_it - wavelet_length);
            if (d_it < lt && d_it >= 0) 
            {
                f_value = 1.0f;//source_func[f_it];
                d_value = shot_recording_arr[d_it];
                
                if (division_mark!=0) 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 / (A4 + stable_coeff) * f_value * d_value;
                } 
                else 
                {
                    tmp1 += A3 * A4 * f_value * d_value;
                }
            }
        }
        
        //migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
        //migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;

        migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale2;
        migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = tmp1 * scale1;
    }
}










//Hessian_KK     = 1/K1  * 1/K2 * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4 * f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4);
//Hessian_Krou   = 1/K1  * 1/K2 * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4* f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4) * cos(2 * \cita_y);
//Hessian_rourou = 1/K1  * 1/K2 * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4* f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4) * cos(2 * \cita_x)* cos(2 * \cita_y);
//Hessian_rouK   = 1/K1  * 1/K2 * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4* f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4) * cos(2 * \cita_x);
// if(para_dependent_compensate_mark==0)
//                 {
//                     k_x = 1.0f;
//                     k_y = 1.0f;	
//                 }

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_multi_parameter_hessian_ND(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 

    int lt, 
    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 


    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 


    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power, 

    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff, 

    int imaging_condition_type, 
    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,  
    float *hessian1,  
    float *hessian2, 
    float *hessian3,  
    float *hessian4, 

    int wx, 
    int wy, 
    int wz, 
    int wxwywz, 

    int count_x, 
    int count_y, 
    int z_dir_speedup_ratio, 
    int num_wxwywz,

    int samplingx,
    int samplingy,
    int samplingz,
    
    int part_start_x,
    int part_start_y,
    int part_start_z,

    int ray_dims
) 
{
    
    int ii = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int jj = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    //// //  out_idx= ix*wx*wz + iwx*wz + iwz;
    int out_idx;
    out_idx = jj * wxwywz + ii;
        
    if (ii < wxwywz && jj <num_wxwywz)
    {
        // ii = iwz * wx * wy + iwy * wx + ix;
        int iwx = ii % wx;                 //  wx index
        int iwy = (ii / wx) % wy;          //  wy index
        int iwz = ii / (wx * wy);          //  wz index
        
        // jj = iz * count_x * count_y + iy * count_x + ix;
        int ix = jj % count_x;
        int iy = (jj / count_x) % count_y;
        int iz = jj / (count_x * count_y);
        
        
            // int x_pos;
			// x_pos=hessian_start_x+ix*hessian_interval_x;
        int x_pos;
		x_pos = part_start_x + ix * samplingx;
        
        int y_pos;
        y_pos = part_start_y + iy * samplingy;

        int z_pos;
        z_pos = part_start_z + iz * samplingz;


        if(x_pos<nx && y_pos<ny && z_pos<nz)
        {
                // int in_idx12;
                // in_idx12 = x_pos*nz + z_pos;//the current psf middle point
            int in_idx12;
            in_idx12      = z_pos * nx * ny + y_pos * nx + x_pos; //the current psf middle point

                // id2_x= x_pos+iwx-int(wx/2);
                // id2_z= z_pos+iwz-int(wz/2);//the spread psfs.
                
                // int in_idx34;
                // in_idx34=id2_x*nz + id2_z;
            int id2_x = x_pos + iwx - int(wx/2);
            int id2_y = y_pos + iwy - int(wy/2);
            int id2_z = z_pos + iwz - int(wz/2);

            int in_idx34;
            bool is_within_bounds;

            if(ray_dims==2)
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz);
            }	
            else
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx * ny + id2_y * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_y>=0 && id2_y<ny  && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz );
            }

            //hessian1[out_idx]   = id2_x;
            //hessian2[out_idx]   = id2_y;
            //hessian3[out_idx]   = id2_z;
            //hessian4[out_idx]   = in_idx34;

            if(is_within_bounds)
            {
                float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   
                int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  
                float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   
                int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  //modeling

                float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
                int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
                float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
                int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);//migration

                int T=0;
                int forward_T=0;
                int adjoint_T=0;
                if(imaging_condition_type==0)
                {
                    T = int(abs(T1 + T2 - T3 - T4));
                    
                    forward_T=T1 + T2 - wavelet_length;
                    adjoint_T=T3 + T4 - wavelet_length + wavelet_max_length;
                }
                    
                else
                {
                    T = int(T3 + T4 - T1 - T2 + wavelet_max_length);
                    
                    forward_T=T1 + T2 - wavelet_length;
                    adjoint_T=T3 + T4 - wavelet_length + wavelet_max_length;
                }
                    
                if(A1!=0 && A2!=0 && A3!=0 && A4!=0 && T>=0 && T<wavelet_length && forward_T>=0 && forward_T<lt && adjoint_T>=0 && adjoint_T<lt)
                {
                    //I recommend that I need to apply the judge condition
                    //hesian weight is not 2*angle_x, there is a big mistake for this, because it should be cos ciat1 *cos ciat2/vx/vy
                    
                    float angle_x;
                    float angle_y;
                    
                    angle_x = fabs(half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34]);
                    angle_y = fabs(half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12]);

                    float scale_anlge_x=1.0f;/// this an half_angle_x
                    float scale_anlge_y=1.0f;/// this an half_angle_x
                    scale_anlge_x = powf(1.0f*cos( 2.0f * angle_x * pai/180.0), 1.0f);
                    scale_anlge_y = powf(1.0f*cos( 2.0f * angle_y * pai/180.0), 1.0f);/// 2 times for born, one times for kirchhoff

                    float k_x, k_y, scale=1.0;
                    if(para_dependent_compensate_mark!=0)
                    {
                        k_x = p_vel_arr[in_idx34]*p_vel_arr[in_idx34]*den_arr[in_idx34];
                        k_y = p_vel_arr[in_idx12]*p_vel_arr[in_idx12]*den_arr[in_idx12];

                        scale = 1.0f/k_x * 1.0f/k_y;
                    }

                    float scale_k_k;
                    float scale_k_rou;
                    float scale_rou_rou;
                    float scale_rou_k;

                    scale_k_k     = 1.0f *scale    * 1.0f;
                    scale_k_rou   = 1.0f *scale    * scale_anlge_y;
                    scale_rou_k   = 1.0f *scale    * scale_anlge_x;
                    scale_rou_rou = 1.0f *scale    * scale_anlge_x * scale_anlge_y;

                    float A=0.0f;
                    if(division_mark==0)	
                        A = 1.0f * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4 * source_func[T];
                    else
                        A = 1.0f * A1 * A2 * A3 / (A4 + 1.0f*stable_coeff) * source_func[T];


                    //if(hes_illumination_matrix_bool==0)
                    {
                            ///////////////k_k
                            hessian1[out_idx]   = A * scale_k_k;
                            //////////////k_rou
                            hessian2[out_idx]   = A * scale_k_rou;
                            //////////////rou_k
                            hessian3[out_idx]   = A * scale_rou_k;
                            //////////////rou_rou
                            hessian4[out_idx]   = A * scale_rou_rou;
                    }
                    // else
                    // {
                    //     if(hes_illumination_matrix_bool==1)
                    //     {
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian1[out_idx], A * scale_k_k);
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian2[out_idx], A * scale_k_rou);
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian3[out_idx], A * scale_rou_k);
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian4[out_idx], A * scale_rou_rou);
                    //     }
                    //     else
                    //     {
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian1[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_k_k));
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian2[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_k_rou));
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian3[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_rou_k));
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian4[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_rou_rou));
                    //     }
                    // }
                    //atomicAdd 适用于 全局内存（global memory）和共享内存（shared memory），但不能用于寄存器变量（registers）
                }
            }
        }
    }
}



//Hessian_kirchhoff1  = 2/v_x * 2/v_y * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4 * f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4);
//Hessian_kirchhoff2  = 2/v_x * 2/v_y * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4 * f(t-T1-T2+T3+T4) * cos(\cita_x)* cos(\cita_y);
// if there is no para_dependent_compensate_mark, the scale is 1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_kirchhoff_hessian_ND(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    int wavelet_max_length, 

    int lt, 
    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 


    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power, 

    int division_mark, 
    float stable_coeff, 

    int imaging_condition_type, 
    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,  
    float *hessian1,  
    float *hessian2, 
    float *hessian3,  
    float *hessian4, 

    int wx, 
    int wy, 
    int wz, 
    int wxwywz, 

    int count_x, 
    int count_y, 
    int z_dir_speedup_ratio, 
    int num_wxwywz,

    int samplingx,
    int samplingy,
    int samplingz,
    
    int part_start_x,
    int part_start_y,
    int part_start_z,

    int ray_dims
) 
{
    
    int ii = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int jj = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    //// //  out_idx= ix*wx*wz + iwx*wz + iwz;
    int out_idx;
    out_idx = jj * wxwywz + ii;
    


    if (ii < wxwywz && jj <num_wxwywz)
    {
        // ii = iwz * wx * wy + iwy * wx + ix;
        int iwx = ii % wx;                 //  wx index
        int iwy = (ii / wx) % wy;          //  wy index
        int iwz = ii / (wx * wy);          //  wz index
        
        // jj = iz * count_x * count_y + iy * count_x + ix;
        int ix = jj % count_x;
        int iy = (jj / count_x) % count_y;
        int iz = jj / (count_x * count_y);
        
        
            // int x_pos;
			// x_pos=hessian_start_x+ix*hessian_interval_x;
        int x_pos;
		x_pos = part_start_x + ix * samplingx;
        
        int y_pos;
        y_pos = part_start_y + iy * samplingy;

        int z_pos;
        z_pos = part_start_z + iz * samplingz;


        if(x_pos<nx && y_pos<ny && z_pos<nz)
        {
                // int in_idx12;
                // in_idx12 = x_pos*nz + z_pos;//the current psf middle point
            int in_idx12;
            in_idx12      = z_pos * nx * ny + y_pos * nx + x_pos; //the current psf middle point       

                // id2_x= x_pos+iwx-int(wx/2);
                // id2_z= z_pos+iwz-int(wz/2);//the spread psfs.
                
                // int in_idx34;
                // in_idx34=id2_x*nz + id2_z;
            int id2_x = x_pos + iwx - int(wx/2);
            int id2_y = y_pos + iwy - int(wy/2);
            int id2_z = z_pos + iwz - int(wz/2);

            int in_idx34;
            bool is_within_bounds;

            if(ray_dims==2)
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz);
            }	
            else
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx * ny + id2_y * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_y>=0 && id2_y<ny  && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz );
            }

            //hessian1[out_idx]   = id2_x;
            //hessian2[out_idx]   = id2_y;
            //hessian3[out_idx]   = id2_z;
            //hessian4[out_idx]   = in_idx34;

            if(is_within_bounds)
            {
                float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   
                int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  
                float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   
                int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  //modeling

                float A3 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx34];
                int T3 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);
                float A4 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx34];
                int T4 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);//migration
                

                int T=0;
                int forward_T=0;
                int adjoint_T=0;
                if(imaging_condition_type==0)
                {
                    T = int(abs(T1 + T2 - T3 - T4));
                    
                    forward_T=T1 + T2 - wavelet_length;
                    adjoint_T=T3 + T4 - wavelet_length + wavelet_max_length;
                }
                    
                else
                {
                    T = int(T1 + T2 - T3 - T4 + wavelet_max_length);
                    
                    forward_T=T1 + T2 - wavelet_length;
                    adjoint_T=T3 + T4 - wavelet_length + wavelet_max_length;
                }
                    
                if(A1!=0 && A2!=0 && A3!=0 && A4!=0 && T>=0 && T<wavelet_length && forward_T>=0 && forward_T<lt && adjoint_T>=0 && adjoint_T<lt)
                {
                    //hesian weight is not 2*angle_x, there is a big mistake for this, because it should be cos ciat1 *cos ciat2/vx/vy
                    
                    float angle_x;
                    float angle_y;
                    
                    angle_x = fabs(half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34]);
                    angle_y = fabs(half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12]);

                    float scale_anlge_x=1.0f;/// this an half_angle_x
                    float scale_anlge_y=1.0f;/// this an half_angle_x
                    scale_anlge_x = powf(1.0f*cos( 1.0f * angle_x * pai/180.0), 1.0f);
                    scale_anlge_y = powf(1.0f*cos( 1.0f * angle_y * pai/180.0), 1.0f);/// 2 times for born, one times for kirchhoff

                    float k_x, k_y, scale=1.0f;  ///1.0f
                    if(para_dependent_compensate_mark!=0)
                    {
                        k_x = p_vel_arr[in_idx34];
                        k_y = p_vel_arr[in_idx12];

                        scale = 4.0f / k_x / k_y;
                    }

                    float scale_k_k;

                    float scale_rou_rou;

                    scale_k_k     = 1.0f *scale    * 1.0f;

                    scale_rou_rou = 1.0f *scale    * scale_anlge_x * scale_anlge_y;

                    float A=0.0f;
                    if(division_mark==0)
                        A = 1.0f * A1 * A2 * A3 * A4  * source_func[T];
                    else
                        A = 1.0f * A1 * A2 * A3 / (A4 + 1.0f*stable_coeff) * source_func[T];
                    
                    //if(hes_illumination_matrix_bool==0)
                    {
                            ///////////////k_k
                            //hessian1[out_idx]   = A * scale_k_k;

                            //hessian2[out_idx]   = A * scale_rou_rou;
                            
                            hessian1[out_idx]   = A * scale_rou_rou;

                            hessian2[out_idx]   = A * scale_k_k;
                    }
                    // else
                    // {
                    //     if(hes_illumination_matrix_bool==1)
                    //     {
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian1[out_idx], A * scale_rou_rou);
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian2[out_idx], A * scale_k_k);
                    //     }
                    //     else
                    //     {
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian1[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_rou_rou) );
                    //         atomicAdd(&hessian2[out_idx], fabsf(A * scale_k_k)     );
                    //     }
                        
                    // }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_hessian_tapering_ND(
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power, 
    float angle_end,


    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,  
    float *hessian,  


    int wx, 
    int wy, 
    int wz, 
    int wxwywz, 

    int count_x, 
    int count_y, 
    int z_dir_speedup_ratio, 
    int num_wxwywz,

    int samplingx,
    int samplingy,
    int samplingz,
    
    int part_start_x,
    int part_start_y,
    int part_start_z,

    int ray_dims
) 
{
    
    int ii = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int jj = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    //// //  out_idx= ix*wx*wz + iwx*wz + iwz;
    int out_idx = jj * wxwywz + ii;

    if (ii < wxwywz && jj <num_wxwywz)
    {
        // ii = iwz * wx * wy + iwy * wx + ix;
        int iwx = ii % wx;                 //  wx index
        int iwy = (ii / wx) % wy;          //  wy index
        int iwz = ii / (wx * wy);          //  wz index
        
        // jj = iz * count_x * count_y + iy * count_x + ix;
        int ix = jj % count_x;
        int iy = (jj / count_x) % count_y;
        int iz = jj / (count_x * count_y);
        
        
            // int x_pos;
			// x_pos=hessian_start_x+ix*hessian_interval_x;
        int x_pos;
		x_pos = part_start_x + ix * samplingx;
        
        int y_pos;
        y_pos = part_start_y + iy * samplingy;

        int z_pos;
        z_pos = part_start_z + iz * samplingz;


        if(x_pos<nx && y_pos<ny && z_pos<nz)
        {
                // int in_idx12;
                // in_idx12 = x_pos*nz + z_pos;//the current psf middle point
            int in_idx12;
            in_idx12      = z_pos * nx * ny + y_pos * nx + x_pos; //the current psf middle point
            
                // id2_x= x_pos+iwx-int(wx/2);
                // id2_z= z_pos+iwz-int(wz/2);//the spread psfs.
                
                // int in_idx34;
                // in_idx34=id2_x*nz + id2_z;
            int id2_x = x_pos + iwx - int(wx/2);
            int id2_y = y_pos + iwy - int(wy/2);
            int id2_z = z_pos + iwz - int(wz/2);

            int in_idx34;
            bool is_within_bounds;

            if(ray_dims==2)
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz);
            }	
            else
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx * ny + id2_y * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_y>=0 && id2_y<ny  && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz );
            }

            if(is_within_bounds)
            {
                // copy from map migrated image into angle domain
                // Get the half scattering angle
                float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];

                // Tapering the migrated image based on the angle
                if (angle_tapering_power != 0.0f) 
                {
                    if (half_opening_angle34 <= angle_start || half_opening_angle34 >= angle_end) 
                    {
                        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), angle_tapering_power);  ///now we use half_opening_angle34
                        hessian[out_idx] *= angle_scale;
                    }
                } 
                else 
                {
                    // if angle_tapering_power ==0, Cut the migrated image if outside the angle range
                    if (half_opening_angle34 <= angle_start || half_opening_angle34 >= angle_end) 
                    {
                        hessian[out_idx] = 0.0f;
                    }
                }

            }
        }
    }
}


//see orignal kernel, we need to note that we should use index: angle_out_idx=angle_id34 * wxwywz * num_wxwywz + out_idx;
//__global__ void cuda_map_psfs_to_angle_domain_final_diag_2(float *num_psf_angle_d,float *num_psf_d,int ex_nx,int nx,int nz,int m_x_start,int m_x_end,int nx_number,int hessian_start_x,int hessian_interval_x,int nz_number,int hessian_start_z,int hessian_interval_z,int wx,int wz,int z_pos,float *angle_d,float angle_start,float dangle,int angle_num,float zeros_angle_weight,int angle_grid_point,float angle_sigma,float hessian_angle_sigma,int mark)

// self.ray_kernel2d_dict['cuda_map_hessian_into_angle_domain_ND'](grid_hessian, block_hessian,    (
// half_scattering_angle_d, angle_start, angle_interval, angle_num, angle_sigma, angle_tapering_power, nx,  ny, nz,  hessian1, wx, wy, wz, wxwywz, count_x,  count_y,  z_dir_speedup_ratio,  num_wxwywz, samplingx, samplingy, samplingz, part_start_x, part_start_y, part_start_z, ray_dims, angle_hessian1, cp.int32(1), cp.int32(add_mark) ), ); 
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_map_hessian_into_angle_domain_ND_7D(
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power, 

    int wangle,

    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,  
    float *hessian,  


    int wx, 
    int wy, 
    int wz, 
    int wxwywz, 

    int count_x, 
    int count_y, 
    int z_dir_speedup_ratio, 
    int num_wxwywz,

    int samplingx,
    int samplingy,
    int samplingz,
    
    int part_start_x,
    int part_start_y,
    int part_start_z,

    int ray_dims,

    float *angle_hessian,
    int accumulation,
    int add_mark
) 
{
    
    int ii = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int jj = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    //// //  out_idx= ix*wx*wz + iwx*wz + iwz;
    int out_idx;
    out_idx = jj * wxwywz + ii;
    
    if (ii < wxwywz && jj <num_wxwywz)
    {
        // ii = iwz * wx * wy + iwy * wx + ix;
        int iwx = ii % wx;                 //  wx index
        int iwy = (ii / wx) % wy;          //  wy index
        int iwz = ii / (wx * wy);          //  wz index
        
        // jj = iz * count_x * count_y + iy * count_x + ix;
        int ix = jj % count_x;
        int iy = (jj / count_x) % count_y;
        int iz = jj / (count_x * count_y);
        
        
            // int x_pos;
			// x_pos=hessian_start_x+ix*hessian_interval_x;
        int x_pos;
		x_pos = part_start_x + ix * samplingx;
        
        int y_pos;
        y_pos = part_start_y + iy * samplingy;

        int z_pos;
        z_pos = part_start_z + iz * samplingz;


        if(x_pos<nx && y_pos<ny && z_pos<nz)
        {
                // int in_idx12;
                // in_idx12 = x_pos*nz + z_pos;//the current psf middle point
            int in_idx12;
            in_idx12      = z_pos * nx * ny + y_pos * nx + x_pos; //the current psf middle point

                // id2_x= x_pos+iwx-int(wx/2);
                // id2_z= z_pos+iwz-int(wz/2);//the spread psfs.
                
                // int in_idx34;
                // in_idx34=id2_x*nz + id2_z;
            int id2_x = x_pos + iwx - int(wx/2);
            int id2_y = y_pos + iwy - int(wy/2);
            int id2_z = z_pos + iwz - int(wz/2);

            int in_idx34;
            bool is_within_bounds;

            if(ray_dims==2)
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz);
            }	
            else
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx * ny + id2_y * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_y>=0 && id2_y<ny  && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz );
            }

            if(is_within_bounds)
            {
                // copy from map migrated image into angle domain
                // Get the half scattering angle
                float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];

                // Compute the angle ID
                int angle_id34 = int((half_opening_angle34 - angle_start) / angle_interval) + add_mark;
                float int_angle34 = angle_id34 * angle_interval + angle_start;

                //we must note that the angle_id34 direction for [0, angle_num]
                //for 7 dimension hessian
                bool is_angle_range;

                is_angle_range=(angle_id34 < angle_num && angle_id34 >= 0);

                if (  is_angle_range  )
                {
                    // Compute weight scale based on angle_sigma
                    float weight_scale = 1.0f;
                    if (angle_sigma != 0.0f) 
                    {
                        float scale = half_opening_angle34 - int_angle34;
                        weight_scale = expf(-1.0f * scale * scale / angle_sigma);
                    }

                    int angle_out_idx;
                    
                    angle_out_idx=angle_id34 * wxwywz * num_wxwywz + out_idx;
                     
                    
                    if(accumulation==0)
                        angle_hessian[ angle_out_idx]  = hessian[out_idx] * weight_scale;
                    else
                        angle_hessian[ angle_out_idx] += hessian[out_idx] * weight_scale;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}


//see orignal kernel, we need to note that we should use index: 
// angle_out_idx=angle_id12 * wxwywz * num_wxwywz + out_idx;
// angle_out_idx=angle_out_idx + angle12_angle34_distance*angle_num*wxwywz * num_wxwywz;

//cuda_map_psfs_to_angle_domain_final_4(float *num_psf_angle_d,float *num_psf_d,int ex_nx,int nx,int nz,int m_x_start,int m_x_end,int nx_number,int hessian_start_x,int hessian_interval_x,int nz_number,int hessian_start_z,int hessian_interval_z,int wx,int wz,int z_pos,float *angle_d,float angle_start,float dangle,int angle_num,float zeros_angle_weight,int angle_grid_point,float angle_sigma,float hessian_angle_sigma,int mark)
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_map_hessian_into_angle_domain_ND_8D(
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power, 

    int wangle,

    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,  
    float *hessian,  


    int wx, 
    int wy, 
    int wz, 
    int wxwywz, 

    int count_x, 
    int count_y, 
    int z_dir_speedup_ratio, 
    int num_wxwywz,

    int samplingx,
    int samplingy,
    int samplingz,
    
    int part_start_x,
    int part_start_y,
    int part_start_z,

    int ray_dims,

    float *angle_hessian,
    int accumulation,
    int add_mark
) 
{
    
    int ii = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int jj = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    int half_angle=int(wangle/2);

    //// //  out_idx= ix*wx*wz + iwx*wz + iwz;
    int out_idx;
    out_idx = jj * wxwywz + ii;
    
    if (ii < wxwywz && jj <num_wxwywz)
    {
        // ii = iwz * wx * wy + iwy * wx + ix;
        int iwx = ii % wx;                 //  wx index
        int iwy = (ii / wx) % wy;          //  wy index
        int iwz = ii / (wx * wy);          //  wz index
        
        // jj = iz * count_x * count_y + iy * count_x + ix;
        int ix = jj % count_x;
        int iy = (jj / count_x) % count_y;
        int iz = jj / (count_x * count_y);
        
        
            // int x_pos;
			// x_pos=hessian_start_x+ix*hessian_interval_x;
        int x_pos;
		x_pos = part_start_x + ix * samplingx;
        
        int y_pos;
        y_pos = part_start_y + iy * samplingy;

        int z_pos;
        z_pos = part_start_z + iz * samplingz;


        if(x_pos<nx && y_pos<ny && z_pos<nz)
        {
                // int in_idx12;
                // in_idx12 = x_pos*nz + z_pos;//the current psf middle point
            int in_idx12;
            in_idx12      = z_pos * nx * ny + y_pos * nx + x_pos; //the current psf middle point

                // id2_x= x_pos+iwx-int(wx/2);
                // id2_z= z_pos+iwz-int(wz/2);//the spread psfs.
                
                // int in_idx34;
                // in_idx34=id2_x*nz + id2_z;
            int id2_x = x_pos + iwx - int(wx/2);
            int id2_y = y_pos + iwy - int(wy/2);
            int id2_z = z_pos + iwz - int(wz/2);

            int in_idx34;
            bool is_within_bounds;

            if(ray_dims==2)
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz);
            }	
            else
            {
                in_idx34             =  id2_z * nx * ny + id2_y * nx + id2_x; //loop for psfs
                is_within_bounds =( id2_x>=0 && id2_x<nx && id2_y>=0 && id2_y<ny  && id2_z>=0 && id2_z<nz );
            }

            if(is_within_bounds)
            {
                // copy from map migrated image into angle domain
                // Get the half scattering angle
                float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];
                float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];

                // Compute the angle ID
                int angle_id34 = int((half_opening_angle34 - angle_start) / angle_interval) + add_mark;
                float int_angle34 = angle_id34 * angle_interval + angle_start;

                int angle_id12 = int((half_opening_angle12 - angle_start) / angle_interval) + add_mark;
                

                int angle12_angle34_distance;
				angle12_angle34_distance = angle_id34 - angle_id12  + half_angle;

                //we must note that the angle_id12 direction for [0, angle_num]
                //for 8 dimension hessian
                bool is_angle_range;

                is_angle_range=(  
                    angle_id34>=(angle_id12-half_angle) && 
                    angle_id34<=(angle_id12+half_angle) &&
                    
                    angle12_angle34_distance>=0 &&
                    angle12_angle34_distance<wangle &&

                    angle_id12<angle_num && angle_id12>=0
                     );

                if(is_angle_range)
                {
                    // Compute weight scale based on angle_sigma
                    float weight_scale = 1.0f;
                    if (angle_sigma != 0.0f) 
                    {
                        float scale = half_opening_angle34 - int_angle34;
                        weight_scale = expf(-1.0f * scale * scale / angle_sigma);
                    }

                    int angle_out_idx;
                    
                    //angle_out_idx=angle_id34 * wxwywz * num_wxwywz + out_idx;//there is an approximation
                    angle_out_idx=angle_id12 * wxwywz * num_wxwywz + out_idx;

                    angle_out_idx=angle_out_idx + angle12_angle34_distance*angle_num*wxwywz * num_wxwywz;
                    
                    
                    if(accumulation==0)
                        angle_hessian[ angle_out_idx]  = hessian[out_idx] * weight_scale;
                    else
                        angle_hessian[ angle_out_idx] += hessian[out_idx] * weight_scale;
                    
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_half_open_angle_2D(
    
    float *s_px_d, 
    float *s_pz_d,
    float *r_px_d, 
    float *r_pz_d,
    int nx, 
    int nz, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d,
    float angle_start) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx && iz < nz) 
    {
        // 1D index for the 2D array
        int in_idx = iz * nx + ix;

        // set zeros
        half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = 0.0f;

        // Compute magnitudes
        float magnitude1 = sqrtf(s_px_d[in_idx] * s_px_d[in_idx] + s_pz_d[in_idx] * s_pz_d[in_idx]);
        float magnitude2 = sqrtf(r_px_d[in_idx] * r_px_d[in_idx] + r_pz_d[in_idx] * r_pz_d[in_idx]);

        // Compute psx and psz
        float psx = 0.0f, psz = 0.0f;
        if (magnitude1 != 0.0f) 
        {
            psx = s_px_d[in_idx] / magnitude1;
            psz = s_pz_d[in_idx] / magnitude1;
        }

        // Compute prx and prz
        float prx = 0.0f, prz = 0.0f;
        if (magnitude2 != 0.0f) 
        {
            prx = r_px_d[in_idx] / magnitude2;
            prz = r_pz_d[in_idx] / magnitude2;
        }

        // Compute the opening angle
        float radian_pp = (magnitude1 != 0.0f && magnitude2 != 0.0f) ? (psx * prx + psz * prz) : 0.0f;
        
        float opening_angle = 0.0f;
        if (fabsf(radian_pp) <= 1.0f) 
        {
            opening_angle = acosf(radian_pp) * 180.0f / pi / 2.0f;
        } else 
        {
            opening_angle = 179.9f / 2.0f;
        }

        // Set the value in half_scattering_angle_d
        half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = opening_angle;

        // Apply angle_start condition
        if (angle_start < 0.0f) 
        {
            float normal_x = prx + psx;
            float normal_z = prz + psz;

            float scale = normal_z * psx - normal_x * psz;

            if (scale < 0.0f) 
            {
                half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = -opening_angle;
            }
        }
    }
}



extern "C" __global__ void cuda_tapering_mig_by_limit_or_cos_angle_1D(
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    int nx, 
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_end, 
    float angle_tapering_power
) 
{
    // Get 2D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    // Compute the 1D index for the 2D array
    int in_idx34 = ix;

    if (ix < nx)
    {
        // Get the half scattering angle
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];

        // Tapering the migrated image based on the angle
        if (angle_tapering_power != 0.0f) 
        {
            if (half_opening_angle34 <= angle_start || half_opening_angle34 >= angle_end) 
            {
                float angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle34 * pi / 180.0f), angle_tapering_power);  ///now we use half_opening_angle34
                migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] *= angle_scale;
            }
        } 
        else 
        {
            // if angle_tapering_power ==0, Cut the migrated image if outside the angle range
            if (half_opening_angle34 <= angle_start || half_opening_angle34 >= angle_end) 
            {
                migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = 0.0f;
            }
        }
    }
}



//__global__ void cuda_maping_offset_image_into_angle_image_func_min(float *output,float *input,int nx,int nz,float  angle_start,float dangle,int angle_num,float *true_opening_angle_d,int nx_append,int nz_append,int up,int left,float zeros_angle_weight,float angle_sigma,int accumulation, int add_mark)  ///see   the previous kernel
//ray_kernel2d_dict['cuda_map_image_into_angle_domain_1D'](grid_1D, block_1D, (migrated_image1_d, angle_migrated_image1_d, NxNyNz, half_scattering_angle_d, angle_start, angle_interval, angle_num, angle_sigma, cp.int32(1), cp.int32(add_mark) ), );
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_map_image_into_angle_domain_1D(
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *angle_migrated_image1_d, 

    int nx,  
    
    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num, 
    float angle_sigma, 
    float angle_tapering_power,

    int accumulation,
    int add_mark
) 
{
    // Get 2D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
   
    // Compute the 1D index for the 2D array
    int in_idx34 = ix;

    if (ix < nx) 
    {
        // Get the half scattering angle
        float half_opening_angle34 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx34];

        // Compute the angle ID
        int angle_id34 = int((half_opening_angle34 - angle_start) / angle_interval) + add_mark;
        float int_angle34 = angle_id34 * angle_interval + angle_start;

        if (angle_id34 < angle_num && angle_id34 >= 0)
        {
            // Compute weight scale based on angle_sigma
            float weight_scale = 1.0f;
            if (angle_sigma != 0.0f) 
            {
                float scale = half_opening_angle34 - int_angle34;
                weight_scale = expf(-1.0f * scale * scale / angle_sigma);
            }

            int angle_out_idx = angle_id34 * nx + in_idx34;
            
            if(accumulation==0)
                angle_migrated_image1_d[ angle_out_idx]  = migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] * weight_scale;
            else
                angle_migrated_image1_d[ angle_out_idx] += migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] * weight_scale;

            //如果每个线程都对应一个独立的角度，也就是说每个线程的 angle_id34 是唯一的，线程之间不会共享相同的 angle_id2，那么你可以放心使用普通的加法操作（+=）来更新数组，因为这些线程不会访问和修改相同的内存位置，不会发生数据竞争。
        }
    }
}



//ray_kernel2d_dict['cuda_mig_multi_parameter_1D_test'](grid_1D, block_1D, (lt, s_amp_d, s_time_d, r_amp_d, r_time_d, migrated_image1_d, migrated_image2_d, shot_recording_arr, NxNyNz), ); 
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_mig_multi_parameter_1D_test(

    int lt,

    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 

    
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    float *migrated_image2_d, 


    float *shot_recording_arr, 
    int nx 
)
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    //int iz = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;

    if (ix < nx ) 
    {
        int in_idx34 = ix;

        float A1 = r_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx34]);  ///must be  int, using floor
        float A2 = s_amp_d[in_idx34];
        int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx34]);
        
        int d_it = int(T1 + T2);

        if (d_it>=0 && d_it<lt)
        {
            float d_value = shot_recording_arr[d_it];

            migrated_image1_d[in_idx34] = d_value;
            migrated_image2_d[in_idx34] = d_value;
        }
    }
}

Key: ray_kernel3d, Value: 




__constant__ const float pi =3.141526;
__constant__ const float pai=3.141526;
__constant__ const float share_zero=0;
//all parameter must be float 32 or int 32 so on......
//all parameter is now revised as  zhang geophysics,2025, single author

//all parameter is now revised as  zhang geophysics,2025, single author

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_modeling_multi_parameter_3D(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length, 
    
    int lt, 

    float *total_acc_d, 
    float *s_amp_d, 
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d, 
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    float *born_rel_vel_d, 
    float *born_rel_den_d, 

    int para_dependent_compensate_mark, 
    int it, 
    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz,

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num, 
    float angle_sigma, 
    float angle_tapering_power
) 
{
    // Get the 3D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    // Compute the 1D index for 3D arrays
    int in_idx12 = iz * ny * nx + iy * nx + ix;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        // Load amplitudes and times
        float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Receiver amplitude
        int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Receiver time
        float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Source amplitude
        int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Source time

        // Compute the half opening angle and angle scale
        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];
        float angle_scale = powf(cosf(2.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//this is 2.0f times half_opening_angle12  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2

        // Compute the Born-related term
        float born_rel_K = born_rel_den_d[in_idx12] + 2.0f * born_rel_vel_d[in_idx12];

        // Conditional check for parameter-dependent compensation
        float K = 1.0f;
        if (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) 
        {
            K = p_vel_arr[in_idx12] * p_vel_arr[in_idx12] * den_arr[in_idx12];
        }

        // Compute scaling factors
        float scale1 = born_rel_K / K;
        float scale2 = (born_rel_den_d[in_idx12] / K) * angle_scale;

        // Calculate the time index in the wavelet
        int f_it = int(it - T1 - T2 + wavelet_length);

        // Apply source function if within bounds
        if (f_it < wavelet_length && f_it >= 0) 
        {
            float f_value = source_func[f_it];
            total_acc_d[in_idx12] = A1 * A2 * f_value * (scale1 + scale2);
        }
    }
}


// d = A1 * A2 * f(t-T1-T2) * [    2 * cos(\cita) * R(x, \cita) / vel      ]
// if para_dependent_compensate_mark == 0:  scale=1.0,  that is 2/v=1.0
extern "C" __global__ void cuda_angle_kirchhoff_modeling_3D(
    float *source_func, 
    int wavelet_length,

    int lt,

    float *total_acc_d, 
    float *s_amp_d,
    float *s_time_d, 
    float *r_amp_d,
    float *r_time_d, 
    
    float *p_vel_arr, 
    float *den_arr, 
    float *angle_ref_d, 

    int para_dependent_compensate_mark,
    int it, 
    int nx, 
    int ny,
    int nz, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_interval, 
    int angle_num,
    float angle_sigma,
    float angle_tapering_power,
    int angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool
) 
{
    // Get the 3D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    // Compute the 1D index for 3D arrays
    int in_idx12 = iz * ny * nx + iy * nx + ix;
    int nxnynz=nx*ny*nz;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        // Load values for amplitudes and times
        float A1 = 1.0f*r_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Receiver amplitude
        int T1 = floor(r_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Receiver time
        float A2 = 1.0f*s_amp_d[in_idx12];   // Source amplitude
        int T2 = floor(s_time_d[in_idx12]);  // Source time

        // Compute the half opening angle and angle scale
        float half_opening_angle12 = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx12];

        // Reference value based on angle index
        float angle_scale = 0.0f;
        float ref = 0.0f;

        if(angle_kirchhoff_modeling_bool)
        {
            angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle12 * pi / 180.0f), 1.0f);//this is 1.0f times half_opening_angle12  1+cos(2*cita) = 2cos(cita)^2

            // Determine the angle index
            int i_angle = int((half_opening_angle12 - angle_start) / angle_interval);
            if (i_angle >= 0 && i_angle < angle_num) 
            {
                ref = angle_ref_d[i_angle * nxnynz + in_idx12];  // 3D reference lookup
            }
        } 
        else
        {
            angle_scale = 1.0f;
            ref = angle_ref_d[in_idx12];
        }

        // Parameter-dependent compensation
        float para_scale = 1.0f;
        if (para_dependent_compensate_mark != 0) 
        {
            para_scale = 2.0f / (p_vel_arr[in_idx12]);
        }

        // Calculate the time index in the wavelet
        int f_it = int(it - T1 - T2 + wavelet_length);

        // Apply source function if within bounds
        if (f_it < wavelet_length && f_it >= 0) 
        {
            float f_value = source_func[f_it];

            total_acc_d[ in_idx12 ] = A1 * A2 * f_value * ref * para_scale * angle_scale;
        }
    }
}

extern "C" __global__ void cuda_tapering_mig_by_limit_or_cos_angle_3D(
    float *migrated_image1_d, 
    int nx, 
    int ny,
    int nz,

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start, 
    float angle_end, 
    float angle_tapering_power
) 
{
    // Get 3D thread index
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    // Compute the 1D index for the 3D array
    int in_idx = iz * ny * nx + iy * nx + ix;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz)
    {
        // Get the half scattering angle
        float half_opening_angle = half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx];

        // Tapering the migrated image based on the angle
        if (angle_tapering_power != 0.0f) 
        {
            if (half_opening_angle <= angle_start || half_opening_angle >= angle_end) 
            {
                float angle_scale = powf(cosf(1.0f * half_opening_angle * pi / 180.0f), angle_tapering_power);  ///now we use half_opening_angle
                migrated_image1_d[in_idx] *= angle_scale;
            }
        } 
        else 
        {
            // Cut the migrated image if outside the angle range
            if (half_opening_angle <= angle_start || half_opening_angle >= angle_end) 
            {
                migrated_image1_d[in_idx] = 0.0f;
            }
        }
    }
}












extern "C" __global__ void cuda_cal_half_open_angle_3D(
    
    float *s_px_d, 
    float *s_py_d, 
    float *s_pz_d, 
    float *r_px_d, 
    float *r_py_d, 
    float *r_pz_d, 

    int nx, 
    int ny, 
    int nz, 

    float *half_scattering_angle_d, 
    float angle_start
) 
{
    int ix = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int iy = blockIdx.y * blockDim.y + threadIdx.y;
    int iz = blockIdx.z * blockDim.z + threadIdx.z;

    if (ix < nx && iy < ny && iz < nz) 
    {
        // Compute the 1D index for the 3D array
        int in_idx = iz * ny * nx + iy * nx + ix;

        // set zeros
        half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = 0.0f;

        // Calculate magnitudes
        float magnitude1 = sqrtf(
            s_px_d[in_idx] * s_px_d[in_idx] + 
            s_py_d[in_idx] * s_py_d[in_idx] + 
            s_pz_d[in_idx] * s_pz_d[in_idx]
        );
        
        float magnitude2 = sqrtf(
            r_px_d[in_idx] * r_px_d[in_idx] + 
            r_py_d[in_idx] * r_py_d[in_idx] + 
            r_pz_d[in_idx] * r_pz_d[in_idx]
        );

        // Initialize psx, psy, psz
        float psx = 0.0f, psy = 0.0f, psz = 0.0f;
        if (magnitude1 != 0.0f) 
        {
            psx = s_px_d[in_idx] / magnitude1;
            psy = s_py_d[in_idx] / magnitude1;
            psz = s_pz_d[in_idx] / magnitude1;
        }

        // Initialize prx, pry, prz
        float prx = 0.0f, pry = 0.0f, prz = 0.0f;
        if (magnitude2 != 0.0f) 
        {
            prx = r_px_d[in_idx] / magnitude2;
            pry = r_py_d[in_idx] / magnitude2;
            prz = r_pz_d[in_idx] / magnitude2;
        }

        // Calculate the dot product for the angle between vectors
        float radian_pp = (magnitude1 != 0.0f && magnitude2 != 0.0f) ? 
                          (psx * prx + psy * pry + psz * prz) : 0.0f;

        // Compute the half opening angle
        float opening_angle = (fabsf(radian_pp) <= 1.0f) ? 
                              (acosf(radian_pp) * 180.0f / pi / 2.0f) : 
                              (179.9f / 2.0f);

        // Store the half opening angle
        half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = opening_angle;

        // Apply condition for angle_start
        if (angle_start < 0.0f) 
        {
            float normal_x = prx + psx;
            float normal_z = prz + psz;
            float scale = normal_z * psx - normal_x * psz;

            if (scale < 0.0f) 
            {
                half_scattering_angle_d[in_idx] = -opening_angle;
            }
        }
    }
}
